t-ng-c4167071336=3D"" class=3D"container ng-star-inserted"><!----><!----><i=
mmersive-editor _ngcontent-ng-c4167071336=3D"" data-test-id=3D"docs-block" =
class=3D"docs-content ng-star-inserted" _nghost-ng-c1483666543=3D"" jslog=
=3D"250633;track:generic_click,impression"><div _ngcontent-ng-c1483666543=
=3D"" class=3D"immersive-editor-container"><div _ngcontent-ng-c1483666543=
=3D"" class=3D"immersive-editor markdown stronger" id=3D"null"><div content=
editable=3D"false" translate=3D"no" class=3D"ProseMirror" aria-label=3D"Can=
vas editor" aria-busy=3D"false" data-disable-editing=3D"false"><h1>Applying=
 the Candy Palette to Jekyll Minima</h1><p>This guide explains how to injec=
t your <strong>Candy Palette</strong> color scheme into a fork of the <a hr=
ef=3D"https://github.com/jekyll/minima" title=3D"null">Jekyll Minima theme<=
/a>. Select the method below that corresponds to your Minima version.</p><h=
2>Option A: For Minima v3.x (Modern Theme with Skins &amp; CSS Variables)</=
h2><p>Minima v3.x uses dynamic CSS custom properties mapped under individua=
l layout skins. The cleanest, most native way to apply your theme is to cre=
ate a custom skin.</p><h3>Step 1: Create a Custom Skin File</h3><p>Create a=
 new file in your repository at the following path:
<code>_sass/minima/skins/candy.scss</code></p><p>Add the following code to =
define both a Light and Dark version of your Candy Palette skin:</p><pre><c=
ode>/**
 * DunbarDigital "Candy Palette" Skin for Minima v3.x
 */

// Define color variables
$light-green:     #72F7A0;
$watermelon:      #ED264D;
  -blue-ice:    #7CB8FF;
$royal-gold:      #F9DD5C;
$neon-violet:     #C64DEC;
$jet-black:       #282C34;
$onyx:            #131418;
$black:           #05060A;
$alabaster-grey:  #DEDFE3;
$pale-slate:      #C4C8D2;

// Custom layout properties
:root {
  --brand-color:             #{$watermelon};
  --brand-color-light:       #{$neon-violet};
  --brand-color-dark:        #{$watermelon};
 =20
  --background-color:        #{$bg-primary};
  --code-background-color:   #{$code-bg};

  --text-color:              #{$text-main};
  --meta-color:              #{$pale-slate};
  --link-color:              #{$watermelon};
  --link-color-visited:      #{$neon-violet};
  --link-color-hover:        #{$light-green};

  --border-color-01:         #{$border-main};
  --border-color-02:         #{$border-secondary};
  --border-color-03:         #{$border-tertiary};

  --table-header-bg:         #{$code-bg};
  --table-row-bg-even:       #{$code-bg};
}

/* Light / Dark Mode media adapters */
@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark) {
  :root {
    --background-color:      #{$black};
    --code-background-color: #{$onyx};
    --text-color:            #{$alabaster-grey};
    --meta-color:            #{$pale-slate};
    --border-color-01:       #{$onyx};
    --border-color-02:       #{$jet-black};
    --border-color-03:       #{$onyx};
    --link-color:            #{$light-green};
    --link-color-visited:    #{$baby-blue-ice};
    --link-color-hover:      #{$watermelon};
  }
}

@media (prefers-color-scheme: light) {
  :root {
    --background-color:      #F8F9FA;
    --code-background-color: #{$alabaster-grey};
    --text-color:            #{$jet-black};
    --meta-color:            #{$pale-slate};
    --border-color-01:       #E5E7EB;
    --border-color-02:       #DEDFE3;
    --border-color-03:       #E5E7EB;
    --link-color:            #{$watermelon};
    --link-color-visited:    #{$neon-violet};
    --link-color-hover:      #{$light-green};
  }
}
<br class=3D"ProseMirror-trailingBreak"></code></pre><h3>Step 2: Update <co=
de>_config.yml</code></h3><p>Tell your Jekyll theme to compile using your b=
rand-new skin. Find the <code>minima</code> configurations in your <code>_c=
onfig.yml</code> and set the skin value:</p><pre><code>minima:
  skin: candy
<br class=3D"ProseMirror-trailingBreak"></code></pre><h2>Option B: For Mini=
ma v2.x (Legacy Theme using Sass Variables)</h2><p>In Minima v2.x, colors a=
re managed via Sass variables compiled at build time.</p><h3>Step 1: Modify=
 <code>_sass/minima.scss</code></h3><p>If your fork contains the full <code=
>_sass</code> directories, locate the variable declarations at the top of <=
code>_sass/minima.scss</code> (or <code>_sass/minima/custom-variables.scss<=
/code>) and replace them with your custom color declarations:</p><pre><code=
>// =3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=
=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=
=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=
=3D
// Candy Palette variables for Minima v2.x
// =3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=
=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=
=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D=3D

$light-green:     #72F7A0;
$watermelon:      #ED264D;
$baby-blue-ice:   #7CB8FF;
$royal-gold:      #F9DD5C;
$neon-violet:     #C64DEC;
$jet-black:       #282C34;
$onyx:            #131418;
$black:           #05060A;
$alabaster-grey:  #DEDFE3;
$pale-slate:      #C4C8D2;

// Map Candy Palette to default Minima variables
$brand-color:             $watermelon !default;
$text-color:              $jet-black !default;
$background-color:        #F8F9FA !default;

// Map grey variants for borders and structure
$grey-color:              $pale-slate !default;
$grey-color-light:        $alabaster-grey !default;
$grey-color-dark:         $jet-black !default;

// Override link interactions
$link-color-hover:        $light-green !default;
<br class=3D"ProseMirror-trailingBreak"></code></pre><h3>Step 2: Handling D=
ark Mode in v2.x</h3><p>Because Minima v2.x does not support Dark Mode nati=
vely out of the box, you will need to add a media query at the bottom of yo=
ur main styling sheet <code>assets/main.scss</code> to handle dark-mode ove=
rrides smoothly using your theme tokens:</p><pre><code>@media (prefers-colo=
r-scheme: dark) {
  body {
    background-color: #05060A !important;
    color: #DEDFE3 !important;
  }
  .site-title, .site-header, .site-footer {
    background-color: #131418 !important;
    border-color: #282C34 !important;
    color: #DEDFE3 !important;
  }
  a {
    color: #72F7A0 !important;
    &amp;:visited {
      color: #7CB8FF !important;
    }
    &amp;:hover {
      color: #ED264D !important;
    }
  }
}
<br class=3D"ProseMirror-trailingBreak"></code></pre></div></div><!----></d=
